<script type="text/javascript">

var rlHttpsSwitch = function() {

  function isLoggedInImpl() {
    return document.cookie.match(new RegExp('LOGGEDIN', 'g')) != null;
  }
  
  function ensureHttps() {
    if (window.location.protocol.toLowerCase() == "http:") {
      window.location.replace(location.href.replace(/http:/, "https:"));
    }
  }
  
  return {
    ensureHttps: function() {
      ensureHttps();
    },
    ensureHttpsIfLoggedIn : function() {
      if (self == top){
        if (isLoggedInImpl()) {
          ensureHttps();
        }
      }
    },
    isLoggedIn: function(){
      return isLoggedInImpl();
    },
    parseUrlProtocolRelative : function(url){
      if (typeof(url) === 'undefined'){
        //url undefined
        return url;
      }else if (url.indexOf("/") === 0 && url.indexOf("//") !== 0) {
        //protocol-less relative url, leave it alone
        return url;
      }else if (url.indexOf('http') == 0){
        //protocol absolute set
        return url;
      }else if (window.location.protocol == 'https:'){
        //https context
        return 'https:'+url;
      }else{
        //http context
        return 'http:'+url;
      }
    }
  };
}();
rlHttpsSwitch.ensureHttpsIfLoggedIn();

</script>

   * returns the next core URL (protocol + server)
  */
  function getNextCoreUrlImpl(){
    switch (window.location.protocol) {
      case 'http:':
        return nextCore;
      case 'https:':
        return nextCoreSecure;
      default:
        return '';
    }
  }

  return {
    cookieRegulation: function() { return cookieRegulation; },
    isEditMode: function(){ return modeEdit; },
    isDesignMode: function(){ return modeDesign; },
    isDisabledMode: function(){ return modeDisabled; },
    isPreviewMode: function(){ return modePreview; },
    onWcmModeChanged: function(_mode){ onWcmModeChangedImpl(_mode); },
    isRunningOnAuthorInstance: function(){return false;},
    isRunningOnLocalhostAuthorInstance: function() { return this.isRunningOnAuthorInstance() && window.location.hostname && window.location.hostname.toLowerCase() === 'localhost'; },

    getNextCoreSecureUrl: function() {return nextCoreSecure;},

<script type="text/javascript">
var COMPONENT_LOADER_JS_LINK = 'https://www.bmw.it/bin/bmw/componentLoader.js';
var rlImagePreloader = function() {
  return {

    preloadImage : function(id) {
      var DELAY = 2000;
      var img = new Image();
      var image = jq('#' + id).hide();
  
      var imageClass;
      if (image.attr('class').match(new RegExp('preLoaderBig', 'g'))) {
        imageClass = 'preLoaderBig';
      } else {
        imageClass = 'preLoaderSmall';
      }
  
      var imageSrc = image.attr('src');
      var imgHeight = image.attr('height');
      var imgWidth = image.attr('width');
  
      var preLoaderAnimationMarkup = '<div class="' + imageClass + 'Div' + '"></div>';
      image.after(preLoaderAnimationMarkup);
  
      var preLoaderAnimation = jq('#' + id).next('.' + imageClass + 'Div');
      preLoaderAnimation.css({
        width : imgWidth,
        height : imgHeight
      }).delay(DELAY).fadeIn();
  
      jq(img).load(
          function() {
            preLoaderAnimation.remove();
            image.attr('src', imageSrc).removeClass(imageClass).show();
          }
      ).attr('src', imageSrc);
    },
    
    __init__ : function() {
    }
  };
}();

    getBodyType: function(){return "";},
    getSeriesId: function(){return "";},
    getBrandId: function(){return "BM";},
    getBrandSubbrand: function(){return "brand-bmw";},
    getVariant: function(){return "NO";}
  };
}();

// Set data in the rlContextObject
if(typeof rlContextObject != "undefined") {
  rlContextObject.setSeriesId(cmxData.getSeriesId());
  rlContextObject.setBodyType(cmxData.getBodyType());
  rlContextObject.setModelRangeId(cmxData.getModelRangeId());
  rlContextObject.setBrandSubbrand(cmxData.getBrandSubbrand());
}

</script>
